[SPELL:SPELL_ARCANE_AEGIS_AIRWARD]
 [NAME:Airward]
 [DESCRIPTION:Increase air resistance]
 [SPHERE:Arcane]
 [SCHOOL:Aegis]
 [DISCIPLINE:Abjuration]
 [SUBDISCIPLINE:Ward]
 [LEVEL:2]
 [EFFECT:Resistance Dur]
 [ANNOUNCEMENT:SOURCE invokes arcane arts to ward TARGET against Air magic]
 [SCRIPTS:1]
 [SCRIPT:wrapper -unitSource \\SOURCE_ID -silence [ SILENCE_ALL SILENCE_SPELL SILENCE_ARCANE SILENCE_AEGIS SILENCE_ABJURATION SILENCE_WARD ] -reflect [ REFLECT_ALL REFLECT_SPELL REFLECT_ARCANE REFLECT_AEGIS REFLECT_ABJURATION REFLECT_WARD ] -iclass [ RESIST_MAGIC RESIST_ARCANE RESIST_AEGIS RESIST_ABJURATION RESIST_WARD IMMUNE_MAGIC IMMUNE_ARCANE IMMUNE_AEGIS IMMUNE_ABJURATION IMMUNE_WARD MAGIC_WARD_3 MAGIC_WARD_4 ] -isyndrome [ Airward ] -value [ 550*source.attribute.focus/2000*(100-target.resistance.aegis/2)/100 ] -script [ unit/resistance-change -unit \\TARGET -resistance [ MAGICAL:ELEMENTAL:AIR ] -fixed [ 50 ] -dur \\VALUE_1 -syndrome “Airward” -track ] ]

[SPELL:SPELL_ARCANE_AEGIS_ARCANEWARD]
 [NAME:Arcaneward]
 [DESCRIPTION:Increase arcane resistance]
 [SPHERE:Arcane]

 [SUBDISCIPLINE:Ward]
 [LEVEL:3]
 [EFFECT:]
 [ANNOUNCEMENT:SOURCE places strong wards on TARGET, inhibiting all Arcane magic]
 [SCRIPTS:1]
 [SCRIPT:wrapper -unitSource \\SOURCE_ID -silence [ SILENCE_ALL SILENCE_SPELL SILENCE_ARCANE SILENCE_AEGIS SILENCE_ABJURATION SILENCE_WARD ] -reflect [ REFLECT_ALL REFLECT_SPELL REFLECT_ARCANE REFLECT_AEGIS REFLECT_ABJURATION REFLECT_WARD ] -iclass [ IMMUNE_MAGIC IMMUNE_ARCANE IMMUNE_AEGIS IMMUNE_ABJURATION IMMUNE_WARD MAGIC_WARD_4 ] -isyndrome [ Arcaneward ] -value [ 800*source.attribute.focus/2000*(100-target.resistance.aegis/2)/100 ] -script [ unit/resistance-change -unit \\TARGET -resistance [ MAGICAL:ARCANE:ALL ] -fixed [ 75 ] -dur \\VALUE_1 -syndrome “Arcaneward” -track ] ]

[SPELL:SPELL_ARCANE_AEGIS_ARCANE_ARMOR]
 [NAME:Arcane Armor]
 [DESCRIPTION:Increase physical and arcane resistance]
 [SPHERE:Arcane]
 [SCHOOL:Aegis]
 [DISCIPLINE:Abjuration]
 [SUBDISCIPLINE:Armor]

 [EFFECT:Resistance Dur]

 [SCRIPTS:1]
 [SCRIPT:wrapper -unitSource \\SOURCE_ID -silence [ SILENCE_ALL SILENCE_SPELL SILENCE_ARCANE SILENCE_AEGIS SILENCE_ABJURATION SILENCE_ARMOR ] -iclass [ RESIST_MAGIC RESIST_ARCANE RESIST_AEGIS RESIST_ABJURATION RESIST_ARMOR IMMUNE_MAGIC IMMUNE_ARCANE IMMUNE_AEGIS IMMUNE_ABJURATION IMMUNE_ARMOR MAGIC_ARMOR_3 MAGIC_ARMOR_4 ] -isyndrome [ Arcane Armor ] -value [ 550*source.attribute.focus/2000*(100-target.resistance.aegis/2)/100 ] -script [ unit/resistance-change -unit \\TARGET -resistance [ MAGICAL:ARCANE:ALL PHYSICAL:ALL ] -fixed [ 10 30 ] -dur \\VALUE_1 -syndrome “Arcane Armor” -track ] ]

 [NAME:Arcane Shield]

 [DISCIPLINE:Abjuration]
 [SUBDISCIPLINE:Shield]
 [LEVEL:1]
 [EFFECT:Resistance Dur]
 [ANNOUNCEMENT:SOURCE conjures arcane energy into a shield, protecting them from damage]
 [SCRIPTS:1]
 [SCRIPT:wrapper -unitSource \\SOURCE_ID -silence [ SILENCE_ALL SILENCE_SPELL SILENCE_ARCANE SILENCE_AEGIS SILENCE_ABJURATION SILENCE_SHIELD ] -iclass [ RESIST_MAGIC RESIST_ARCANE RESIST_AEGIS RESIST_ABJURATION RESIST_SHIELD IMMUNE_MAGIC IMMUNE_ARCANE IMMUNE_AEGIS IMMUNE_ABJURATION IMMUNE_SHIELD MAGIC_SHIELD_2 MAGIC_SHIELD_3 MAGIC_SHIELD_4 ] -isyndrome [ Arcane Shield ] -value [ 300*source.attribute.focus/2000*(100-target.resistance.aegis/2)/100 ] -script [ unit/resistance-change -unit \\TARGET -resistance [ MAGICAL:ARCANE:ALL PHYSICAL:ALL ] -fixed [ 15 15 ] -dur \\VALUE_1 -syndrome “Arcane Shield” -track ] ]

[SPELL:SPELL_ARCANE_AEGIS_ARCANE_WALL]
 [NAME:Arcane Wall]
 [DESCRIPTION:Create a wall]
 [SPHERE:Arcane]
 [SCHOOL:Aegis]
 [DISCIPLINE:Invocation]
 [SUBDISCIPLINE:Construct]
 [LEVEL:3]
 [EFFECT:Summon Wall Dur]
 [ANNOUNCEMENT:SOURCE conjures a large wall of pure arcane energy]
 [SCRIPTS:1]
 [SCRIPT:wrapper -unitSource \\SOURCE_ID -silence [ SILENCE_ALL SILENCE_SPELL SILENCE_ARCANE SILENCE_AEGIS SILENCE_INVOCATION SILENCE_CONSTRUCT ] -script [ unit/create -loc \\LOCATION -unit SPELL_CONSTRUCT_WALL:ARCANE -reference \\SOURCE -friendly -dur \\VALUE_1 ] ]

[SPELL:SPELL_ARCANE_AEGIS_ARCANE_WEAPON]
 [NAME:Arcane Weapon]
 [DESCRIPTION:Change weapon material to arcane]
 [SPHERE:Arcane]
 [SCHOOL:Aegis]
 [DISCIPLINE:Transmutation]
 [SUBDISCIPLINE:Artifice]
 [LEVEL:1]
 [EFFECT:Imbue Dur]
 [ANNOUNCEMENT:SOURCE imbues their weapon with arcane energy]
 [SCRIPTS:1]
 [SCRIPT:wrapper -unitSource \\SOURCE_ID -silence [ SILENCE_ALL SILENCE_SPELL SILENCE_ARCANE SILENCE_AEGIS SILENCE_TRANSMUTATION SILENCE_ARTIFICE ] -iclass [ RESIST_MAGIC RESIST_ARCANE RESIST_AEGIS RESIST_TRANSMUTATION RESIST_ARTIFICE IMMUNE_MAGIC IMMUNE_ARCANE IMMUNE_AEGIS IMMUNE_TRANSMUTATION IMMUNE_ARTIFICE MAGIC_WEAPON_2 MAGIC_WEAPON_3 MAGIC_WEAPON_4 ] -isyndrome [ Arcane Weapon ] -ritem [ WEAPON ] -value [ 500*source.attribute.focus/2000 ] -script [ Item/material-change -unit \\TARGET -weapon -mat PLANT_MAT:SPELL_MATERIALS_ARCANE:ARCANE -dur \\VALUE_1 -syndrome “Arcane Weapon” -track ] ]
